how-to-play-guide-inner"><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-q"><div class="title-guide-singles-lol">What Lane Is Lulu?</div><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-inner-ul"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-a">Due to the lane phase of this pick, it is frequently played in the Support position. This pick has yet to see any meaningful play in other lanes.</li></ul></li></ul><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-q"><div class="title-guide-singles-lol">Is Lulu Good Right Now?</div><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-inner-ul"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-a">Ranking as the <span class="role-rank-style-text-lol">#28 Best Pick</span> In the <span class="role-style-text-lol">Support</span> role for patch 11.24, placing it within our <span class="tier-style-text-lol">A-Tier</span> Rank. A good pick for ranking up in solo queue, concerning difficulty, this is a moderately diffcult to play champion for new players in league of legends.</li></ul></li></ul><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-q"><div class="title-guide-singles-lol">How Do I Build Lulu S11 Patch 11.24?</div><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-inner-ul"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-a">Since this season 11 Lulu Build and Runes will help you deal Magic damage, you will be focusing on building support items to help enable your bottom lane carry, either through shield, healing or simiply providing peel.</li></ul></li></ul><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-q"><div class="title-guide-singles-lol">Champions Like Lulu</div><ul class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-inner-ul"><li class="rb-build-sec-desc-guide-single-a">Similar picks regarding playstyle would be Enchanter types. That would include Nami which is a really excellent pick at the moment, as well as Soraka and Janna</li></ul></li></ul><div class="counters-sidebar-sim"><div
